---
title: Public API Changes in Aspose.Imaging 3.8.0
type: docs
weight: 110
url: /net/public-api-changes-in-aspose-imaging-3-8-0/
---

{{% alert color="primary" %}} 

This document describes the changes to the Aspose.Imaging API from version 3.7.0 to 3.8.0 that may be of interest to module/application developers. It includes not only new and updated public methods, [added APIs](/imaging/net/public-api-changes-in-aspose-imaging-3-8-0-html/) and [removed APIs](/imaging/net/public-api-changes-in-aspose-imaging-3-8-0-html/), but also a description of any changes in the behavior behind the scenes in Aspose.Imaging.

{{% /alert %}} 
## **Added Classes, Enumerations and Methods**
Following is the list of classes, methods, enumerations and properties introduced in Aspose.Imaging for .NET 3.8.0:

Class    Aspose.Imaging.[FileFormats](/pages/createpage.action?spaceKey=imagingnet&title=FileFormats&linkCreation=true&fromPageId=14779069).Tiff.[TiffExifIfd](/pages/createpage.action?spaceKey=imagingnet&title=TiffExifIfd&linkCreation=true&fromPageId=14779069)
